User: Count vowels in: "Machine learning algorithms process large datasets"
Assistant: <think>I need to count all vowels (a, e, i, o, u) in the text.</think>
<model>
text = "Machine learning algorithms process large datasets"
vowels = "aeiouAEIOU"
count = sum(1 for char in text if char in vowels)
print(f"Number of vowels: " + str(count))
</model>

User: Calculate the area of a circle with radius 23
Assistant: <think>Area of a circle = π × r². With radius 23, area = π × 23².</think>
<model>
import math
radius = 23
area = math.pi * radius**2
print(f"Area = " + str(round(area, 2)) + " square units")
</model>

User: Calculate area and perimeter of rectangle with length 11 and width 7
Assistant: <think>For a rectangle: Area = length × width, Perimeter = 2(length + width).</think>
<model>
length = 11
width = 7
area = length * width
perimeter = 2 * (length + width)
print(f"Area = " + str(area) + " square units")
print(f"Perimeter = " + str(perimeter) + " units")
</model>

User: Is 156 a prime number?
Assistant: <think>A prime number is only divisible by 1 and itself. I need to check if 156 has any other divisors.</think>
<model>
def is_prime(n):
    if n < 2:
        return False
    for i in range(2, int(n**0.5) + 1):
        if n % i == 0:
            return False
    return True

number = 156
result = is_prime(number)
print(f"156 is " + ("prime" if result else "not prime"))
</model>
<requires>python:math</requires>

156 is not prime.

    return True

Assistant: <think>To convert Celsius to Fahrenheit: F = (C × 9/5) + 32.</think>
<model>
celsius = 36
fahrenheit = (celsius * 9/5) + 32
print(f"36°C = " + str(fahrenheit) + "°F")
</model>

User: I buy 3 books for $17 each and 2 pens for $13 each. How much change from $91?
Assistant: <think>Total cost = (3 × $17) + (2 × $13) = $77. Change = $91 - $77.</think>
<model>
item1_price = 17
item1_qty = 3
item2_price = 13
item2_qty = 2
payment = 91

total_cost = (item1_price * item1_qty) + (item2_price * item2_qty)
change = payment - total_cost
print(f"Total cost: $" + str(total_cost))
print(f"Change: $" + str(change))
</model>
<requires>python:math</requires>

The total cost is $77, so the change from $91 is $14.
